**Q2: For ground truths and predictions, what are their projected functions derived from the combination of sine and cosine functions?**

The ground truths can be modeled using a sine function, but the predictions can be modeled using a cosine function with a phase shift, not just a cosine function.

The sine function for the ground truths can be represented as:

y = A * sin(2 * pi * t / 12 + phi) + B

where A is the amplitude, B is the offset, phi is the phase shift, and t is the time in hours.

The cosine function for the predictions can be represented as:

y = C * cos(2 * pi * t / 12 + psi) + D

where C is the amplitude, D is the offset, psi is the phase shift, and t is the time in hours.
